msg:The biggest surprise of this trip to Dali should be the Mangshu Taotang Hill Sea View Hotel located in Shuanglang!
Location: üìçNo. 108, Dajianpang Village, Shuanglang Town
Although it is some distance from the center of Shuanglang Town, it just feels like being quiet in the middle of the bustle. Because the hotel only has 16 rooms in total, there are not many guests, so we rarely encounter other guests when we go in and out. Overall Privacy is also good

Environment: From the moment I stepped into the lobby, I was attracted by their new Chinese style decoration style, which is simple and high-end. This time the three of us booked the Lujiang Courtyard Family Suite (with two queen beds) Especially suitable for us), the room is quite large, with a huge floor-to-ceiling window. I can imagine how long it will be if the weather is good, I lie on the sofa, the sun shines in, and a cup of latte at the table exudes the aroma. It's quiet and quiet, but it's a pity that it was the rainy season when we went there. There was no sunshine and only endless rain.

Facilities: Although the hotel is small, it is well-equipped with all the supporting facilities that a hotel should have, such as gym, tea room, children's playground, conference room, etc. The room facilities are also excellent, including Marshall audio, Ferragamo washing and care, Dyson hair dryer, and Kohler bathroom. There is also Puna mineral water and Perrier water in the small refrigerator, which are also free, reflecting high quality and good taste everywhere.

Catering: The hotel's breakfast tastes really good. It can be said to be better than many five-star hotels. Although the variety is not rich, it has all the categories. In addition to the buffet, different staple foods are also provided every day. You can choose noodles, Rice noodles or bait wire, etc.
A free afternoon tea with fruits, nuts, cakes and drinks will be provided during your stay.
There is also a different good night sweet soup provided every night. Have a bowl of it when you go home at night, and the fatigue of the day will be wiped away.

Service: Finally, I want to focus on their service! They say that the best service is to give you the feeling of going home, and they do exactly that. The service started before we checked in. The hotel would contact us in advance and inform us of the exclusive butler for our stay. Then we set up a WeChat group. If we have any questions or needs during our stay, we can report them in the group. Whether we are checking in, checking out or any time we appear in the lobby, the service staff will immediately ask if we want tea or coffee, making us feel like we are being taken seriously while waiting; we stayed here for three days in total , our housekeeper is called Xiao Jin, he is a very young and energetic guy. We come in and out many times every day, and Xiao Jin will drive us in his modified car. Although the weather in Dali is a bit cold when it rains, we are still hiding in the car. There is some warmth in my heart. When the car shuttles through the winding alleys of Shuanglang, listening to Xiaojin enthusiastically talking about the various delicious and fun things in Shuanglang, you will find a different kind of beauty at this moment; during your stay As long as we told the housekeeper group that we needed water, a clothes iron, etc., Xiaojin would fulfill our needs as soon as possible; the hotel provided free parking service, but we didn't know it on the first day and paid for the parking ourselves. Xiao Jin immediately apologized to us and reimbursed the parking fee for us as soon as he knew it. He gave us parking tickets in time in the next few days; when we left on the last day, the hotel also gave us a souvenir. It was said that he was a friend of the boss. The ancient tree black tea baked by ourselves, the tea tastes really good. There may be many details that cannot be described one by one in words, but my friend and I agreed that their service was very good during our stay this time. They were sincere and not pretentious, enthusiastic and not hypocritical, making people feel comfortable and at ease!

As the saying goes, the aroma of wine is not afraid of deep alleys. If you come to Dali, don‚Äôt miss this treasure hotel hidden in the corner!

I discovered the benefits of the elevator because I was climbing a mountain and my feet were sprained. 4. Meals are quite satisfactory, maybe there are few people, and the buffet is not used. The hotel provides catering and afternoon tea. What is worthy of praise is that you can make freshly ground American coffee at any time.
The suggestion is to target the audience of the hotel well. The supporting software facilities and value-added services of the hotel will attract more customers. The competition in Dali B&B is very fierce.
